kitmus/background-inference-charfict-real/subtask_3_ents/knowledge-text-only/test:1993
The work of a dandlider is working on a farm usually with animals. Walburn is a dandlider. Villanueva is a cabbier. The work of a cabbier is designing building and houses. Shinault is an orgemier. The work of an orgemier is passing knowledge to students at school.

kitmus/background-inference-charfict-real/subtask_3_ents/knowledge-text-only/test:1994
The work of a johumker is deciding cases in a law court. Colbert is a remaller. Coyle is a johumker. Petersen is a turper. The work of a remaller is working for the army. The work of a turper is unpacking merchandise when it arrives at the warehouse.

The work of an undinger is assisting organizations by performing a variety of clerical functions. Letcher is an undinger. Lichtenstein is a turper.

The work of a dandlider is working on a farm usually with animals. The work of a cabbier is designing building and houses. Renshaw is a cabbier.

kitmus/background-inference-charfict-real/subtask_3_ents/knowledge-text-only/test:1999
Stoltzfus is a cabbier. Sauer is a vegeer. The work of a vegeer is creating and serving alcoholic drinks to patrons at a bar or a restaurant. The work of a quarancer is making things from wood including houses and furniture. Gullett is a quarancer. The work of a cabbier is designing building and houses.
